style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">LLOYD DEAN AND JOHN MULLIGAN ELECTED </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">TO MCDONALD&#8217;S BOARD OF DIRECTORS </font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;text-indent:32px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;text-indent:32px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">OAK BROOK, Ill. - McDonald&#8217;s Corporation today announced its Board of Directors elected Lloyd Dean and John Mulligan as Directors of the company, effective August 3.  </font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;text-indent:32px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Dean, 65, is President and CEO of Dignity Health, where he is responsible for the overall management of Dignity Health&#8217;s hospitals, home health care and medical group foundations.  Since becoming CEO at Dignity Health in 2000, Dean has led the organization through significant strategic, operational and financial transformations to its current status as a leading health care organization. Prior to his current role, Dean was Chief Operating Officer</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#ff0000;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">at Advocate Health Care.  </font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;text-indent:32px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Dean is on the Board at Wells Fargo &amp; Company and Navigant Consulting, Inc. He holds a bachelor&#8217;s degree in Sociology and a master&#8217;s degree in Education from Western Michigan University in Kalamazoo, Mich.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;text-indent:32px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Mulligan, 49, is Executive Vice President and Chief Financial Officer at Target, where he leads financial and retail services, which include the company&#8217;s credit card operations. Mulligan joined Target in 1996 as a Financial Analyst, and during his tenure held key leadership positions in finance, human resources and with Target.com. In 2012, Mulligan was promoted to his current position at Target.&#160;While continuing to act as CFO, he served as interim President and CEO from May to August 2014.</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;text-indent:32px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Mulligan serves on the Minnesota Children&#8217;s Hospitals and Clinics Board.  He earned a bachelor&#8217;s degree from the University of Wisconsin and a Master of Business Administration from the University of Minnesota.</font></div><br><div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:right;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="sEC25D50B97DABC0EFCB8FBE7F3B546BB"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;text-indent:32px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#8220;Both Lloyd and John bring valuable skill sets that are well-suited for our Board,&#8221; said Andrew McKenna, McDonald&#8217;s Chairman of the Board.  &#8220;We&#8217;re delighted to add these talented leaders and leverage their financial and operational expertise.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;text-indent:32px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#8220;We&#8217;re pleased to welcome Lloyd and John to McDonald&#8217;s as we establish ourselves as a modern and progressive burger company,&#8221;
